***лишить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a> (4586)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lišiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*leykʷ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lend</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">loan</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишать.html>лиша́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deprive, to rob, to bereave
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишенный.html>лишены́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>самого</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:корённый.html>коренно́го</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>права</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">oní <b>lišený</b> samovo korennóvo prava</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they are <b>deprived</b> of the most fundamental rights</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to devest, to forjudge, to dispossess
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive / rob (smb.) of his rights</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наследство.html>насле́дства</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> naslédstva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disinherit</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> sebjá žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take one's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>пра́ва</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голос.html>го́лоса</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> práva gólosa</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disfranchise</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:воинский.html>во́инских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:звание.html>зва́ний</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> vóinskix zvánij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to reduce to the ranks</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́ва</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> slóva</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deny (smb.) the right to speak</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:парламентский.html>парла́ментского</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мандат.html>манда́та</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> parlámentskovo mandáta</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to unseat</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:удовольствие.html>удово́льствия</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> sebjá udovólʹstvija</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to deprive oneself</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:духовный.html>духо́вного</a> са́на</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> duxóvnovo sána</i> ― <span class="e-translation">defrock, unfrock</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишить.html>лиши́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гражданский.html>гражда́нских</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:право.html>прав</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišítʹ</b> graždánskix prav</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to disfranchise</span></div></dd>

***лишь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a> (199)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лише</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">liše</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, originally comparative form of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лихъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lixŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bad</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">лише́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lyšé</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lišʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>only, merely, just
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:бы.html>бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišʹ</b> by</i> ― <span class="e-translation">if only</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>as soon as
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:лишь.html>лишь</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lišʹ</b> tólʹko</i> ― <span class="e-translation">no sooner ... than</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:только.html>то́лько</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kak tólʹko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:едва.html>едва́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jedvá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lъbъ</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*lubʰo</i>.

<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лоб.html>лоб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lob</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ан</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-an</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***ловить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a> (1832)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lovìti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to (try to) catch</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lovítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поймать.html>пойма́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:изловить.html>излови́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to catch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lovítʹ</b> rýbu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to catch fish</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a> (5573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*lovъkъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvkij</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ловче́е</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)<a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ловче́й</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)ло́вче</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>adroit, dexterous, deft</li>
<li>cunning, smart, crafty, never at a loss</li>
<li>comfortable</li></ol>

***ловко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a> (2630)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóvkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>skillfully, artfully, knowingly</li>
<li>neatly</li>
<li>cunningly, shrewdly, slick</li>
<li>trippingly</li>
<li>nattily</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловко.html>ло́вко</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvko</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lóvkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***ловчий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a> (14925)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-чий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-čij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvčij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>hunting
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:птица.html>пти́цы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lóvčije</b> ptícy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">hunting birds</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>serving as a snare/trap
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ров.html>ров</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>lóvčij</b> rov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">trap</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловить.html>лови́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lovítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловля.html>ло́вля</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lóvlja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловец.html>лове́ц</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lovéc</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловкий.html>ло́вкий</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">lóvkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lóvčij</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчего</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчие</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ловчий.html>ло́вчих</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> huntsman, master of hounds</li></ol>

***лодка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a> (1257)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лодъка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lodŭka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, diminutive of <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">лодья</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">lodĭja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oldī</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">lódka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́док</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>boat, dinghy, gig, yawl</li></ol>
